Notification from the Ministry of Industry to the Chamber of Commerce Regarding the Promotion of Domestic Timber 206

Drafted by the public works departments of various provinces and cities.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, citing the massive import of foreign pine in recent years and the declining sales of domestic pine, had resolved at its fifth delegate assembly to petition the National Government's Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, etc., to find ways to provide relief in order to maintain domestic timber, etc. It is now learned that the Ministry of Industry yesterday notified the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating that the application of domestic construction timber has been repeatedly ordered by the government and has been duly recorded. Regarding the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's original request to establish regulations, stipulating that in the future, all construction must adhere to the use of a certain proportion of domestic fir timber before licenses are issued, this matter falls under the jurisdiction of the public works departments of various provinces and cities. The provincial and municipal governments should be instructed to consider local conditions and draft implementation measures to be submitted to the ministry for record-keeping and compliance, aiming for standardization. However, it has been found that domestic timber has not yet been tested for its modulus of elasticity, elastic strength, breaking strength, etc., making it impossible to understand its properties. Furthermore, there is no standard for dimensions, causing great inconvenience in its use. Improvements are urgently needed. The Ministry's Central Industrial Testing Laboratory has equipment for timber testing. Industry guilds from various timber producing areas should submit samples to the laboratory for testing and guidance on standard timber extraction methods to meet the needs of modern construction. A copy of the letter and the original request are being forwarded to various provincial and municipal governments for handling, and instructions are being issued to the Central Industrial Testing Laboratory for compliance. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce is being notified accordingly.

Dispute Over House Demolition in Leyi Lane, French Concession 207

Tenants Held a General Meeting Yesterday to Firmly Oppose

The houses in Leyi Lane, Nanyang Bridge, Avenue Anna King, French Concession, totaling thirty to forty buildings, were built only fourteen or fifteen years ago. The buildings are sturdy and there is no need for reconstruction. In June of this year, the landlord, Jiang Hanzhai, suddenly cited reconstruction as a reason. Upon hearing the news, the tenants elected representatives to negotiate with the landlord. As a result, the landlord agreed to a postponement, and the Tillback Real Estate Department announced a one-year extension, but with a 30% rent increase and payment of all outstanding rent. Otherwise, reconstruction would proceed as planned. While the tenants were preparing to negotiate with the landlord regarding the rent increase and extension period, they suddenly received a notice from the Tillback Real Estate Department canceling the previous agreement and deciding to proceed with reconstruction, requiring all tenants to vacate the premises before September 30th. The tenants unanimously opposed this move by the landlord and sent a letter to the Fourth Branch of the Second Special District Municipal Federation requesting them to send representatives to mediate with the landlord for a final time on the previous day. It is now reported that the mediation by the Federation has yielded no results, with the landlord's attitude remaining firm and leaving no room for negotiation. The tenants then held a general meeting of all tenants at the Citizen's Hall inside the Anxin Temple at 8 PM yesterday to discuss resolute countermeasures. More than forty tenants attended, and Dong Wenli and Ye Ruizhai, standing committee members of the Fourth District Municipal Federation, attended to report on the mediation with the landlord and provide guidance. Li Yuting chaired the meeting, and Yu Jingqing served as the recorder. After the report, the following countermeasures were resolved: (1) All stood up and unanimously expressed their determination to refuse to vacate the premises under any pressure; (2) Engage Wu Kaisheng and Zhu Dianqing, two prominent lawyers, as legal advisors to provide legal protection; (3) Immediately establish the Leyi Lane branch of the Fourth Branch of the Citizen's Association, with Li Yuting, Wang Dekui, and Tang Baoshan as officers responsible for negotiations and reporting to higher authorities for record-keeping; (4) Collect different notices posted by the landlord at the entrance of the lane and those issued by the rental department, as well as all other evidence, and submit them to the party and government authorities to seek justice and prevent the demolition of the houses in order to maintain social order; (5) Send letters to various organizations to appeal for united assistance; (6) Issue a declaration detailing the history of oppression and requesting all sectors to rise up and provide assistance; (7) Print and distribute slogans to show determination; (8) Implement the signing of covenants to prevent breaches and urge all households to deposit their outstanding rent; (9) Stipulate that each building should contribute ten yuan for all negotiation expenses. All of the above measures were passed unanimously, and the meeting was adjourned.

How to Strive in Reading and Answering Questions 218

|| Answer to Mr. Zhang Yiyan

Not long ago, this column published an article discussing "Private Life and Ideals." That piece was triggered by two other articles, one being "On the Contradictions of Life" and the other "Explaining Practice." Mr. Zhang’s letter stated that after reading "Private Life and Ideals" and examining his own private life, he had many doubts. Mr. Zhang believes this is "a common ailment suffered by many people," which he "cannot overcome, like the surging waves of youthful melancholy." We have also seen this for a long time.

It seems Mr. Zhang has not truly grasped the important points of "Private Life and Ideals." That article was a continuation of the two articles mentioned earlier. Our emphasis was only on the point that private life should be consistent with ideals. Because we often see people with high ideals but deplorable private lives, they only have ideals but ultimately cannot realize them. Therefore, we specifically raised this point to answer Mr. Xiao and Mr. Luo. As for how to achieve this, we can only offer principles and methods, not detailed specifics of the process. Because that is impossible. Everyone has their own life practices and ideals. How can you plan for others? Mr. Zhang thinks the word "striving" is "too difficult for people to understand" and "suspects that the word 'striving' is just a comforting word, like stuffing a piece of candy in the mouth of a crying child." This is a complete misunderstanding of the scientific method of managing one's life. Regarding the "Private Life and Ideals" article, we deliberately omitted this part because we had already said a little in the "On the Contradictions of Life" and "Explaining Practice" articles. Mr. Zhang may not have read those two short essays!

Below, we will further discuss with Mr. Zhang the three questions he raised. The first is about sex, the second is about the way out of life, and the third is about stimulation. Mr. Zhang considers these three questions "the biggest cause of youth's depression, hindering their progress, and destroying their will." To be honest, we cannot completely agree.

We believe that a youth with a correct worldview, social view, and outlook on life, who already has correct ideals, his private life will gradually approach his ideals day by day and will never deviate too far. As long as he understands the contradictory nature of life itself, he will not see life as a fixed, static state. He will not fear the contradictions of life, succumb to the contradictions that contradict his ideals, nor will he deliberately hide the contradictions in his life, fearing that others will see them. A person who does not shy away from practice has the perseverance to face all hardships. He is very serious about the struggle in his private life and is unwilling to relax even a little. Like the three questions raised by Mr. Zhang, the first one does occupy a more important position in the private life of young people. However, it is not as extreme as Mr. Zhang said. Generally, sexual depression leading to "being foolish" and "bored" all day long is only a few, all of the molecules in the social level are not the general public. But this does not deny the sexual needs of young people. The sexual desires of young people are very normal. We believe that a person who practices can naturally solve it according to their living conditions. All problems can only be solved in practice. But don't exaggerate this problem too much. When Mr. Zhang encounters sexual desires, he "sits in boredom for a day." This is because Mr. Zhang's life is still relatively leisurely, so the method of solving it is also leisurely. However, Mr. Zhang has not solved the problem. Sexual climaxes come and go, and then he has to adopt "sitting in boredom for a day." May I ask, is this still a life lived by a human being? If we want to talk about a reluctant solution to this problem, it is the same as the life problem we will talk about below. In this "death," we advocate a compromise solution, that is, when you can marry, don't demand too much in terms of the partner, and simplify the sexual problem. When you can't marry, use work, labor, etc. to reduce its attacks, not "sitting in boredom." Because the problem of sex is ultimately secondary to food. You won't starve to death without a wife. Naturally, this is not a true solution to the problem. This problem is a social problem and cannot be completely solved by an individual alone. A young man with ideals will not be depressed by these problems and destroy his own will because he knows it is completely useless. And if you exaggerate this kind of contradiction in life too much, although you "dare not degenerate," in fact, being in "annoyance" all day long, unable to move forward, is no different from degenerating, is it? (To be continued)

Chunqiu

Little Western Paradise 219

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 1: Ghosts Carry a Cart of Distant Guests from Guanzhong; Destitute Families Cross the Ferry and Mourn the Qin People

Zhang Jiefu said: Actually, we are not that old. As long as we find a better job, we can leave after a year or two. Enduring a bit of hardship doesn't matter much. Li Shilian had nothing to say but sighed. In their extremely aggrieved situation, the car drove to the bottom of the Xi’an city. According to the rules, there was an inspection at the city gate before being allowed to pass. Both Zhang and Li were visiting Xi’an for the first time and immediately began to pay attention after entering the city. The most striking difference from the East is that everything is light yellow. The walls of the houses are all built of yellow earth, absolutely without any paint. The soil on the streets is not as jet-black as in the East but has a grayish-yellow tinge. Even the tiles on the roofs seem somewhat yellow, probably due to the dust blown onto them, covering them with a layer of yellow. The car turned two corners on such a wide street and headed onto a main street. Although this street was also seventy or eighty feet wide, it was entirely a dirt road. Some shops with wooden-floored buildings were also tilting and falling. Most of the shops still looked like the old towns in the East forty or fifty years ago. Some had a square wooden stall propped up at the entrance, some hung strings of paper tassels under the eaves, and some hung square blue cloth signs with red lettering in the middle. As the two of them were admiring the scene, the car stopped. Looking up, they saw a high wall of an earthen warehouse next to the road, with a one-character door frame under it. Above the door was a horizontal plaque with three large characters: Little Western Paradise. Looking inside the door, there was a counter on the left and a large signboard on the wooden wall on the right, which was the place for travelers to register their names. Seeing this situation, it was quite like a small inn in the interior of the Yangtze River. He asked Wang Laowu: Is this the best hotel in Xi’an city? Wang Laowu said: If you want to find a cheaper hotel than this, there are many. You can call a rickshaw to take you there. Zhang Jiefu said: If there are hotels smaller than this, how can we live? Okay, then let's stay at Little Western Paradise. (Eight)

The Examination Candidate and the Old Examination Candidate Sun Yucai 220

My younger cousin came to take the entrance examination at XX Middle School. On the day of the exam, he asked me to send him there.

As the morning sun rose, two rickshaws pulled up to the school gate. Walking in, the playground, corridors, and open spaces were already filled with many examination candidates.

Most of these examination candidates came from the rural areas of the interior, so very few of them were dressed in Western style, and no more than one-third wore leather shoes. But they all had a long gown, made of Hangzhou silk, official gauze, summer cloth, gauze, and silk, but I didn't see any thin silk gauze.

Among these many young examination candidates, there were quite a few old men over forty or fifty years old, wearing blue cloth shoes, white cloth socks, and a short summer cloth jacket and pants, also white. Some wore old straw hats that had turned black, some wore patched summer cloth long gowns, some had a pair of copper-rimmed glasses on their eyes, and some wore foreign socks instead of cloth socks, which were probably newly bought. It is said that these are all the fathers of the examination candidates, the old examination candidates. It was still early, and everyone was pacing, with humorous expressions on their faces. On one side of the grape trellis, I heard an examination candidate and an old examination candidate talking:

"………This time, it was your mother who was willing to exchange some gold jewelry, otherwise you would have to help out in your uncle's shop; if the situation doesn't change, we can't think about the future.………I don't expect anything from you, just want you to be like Chunping in Dongcun, graduate and work in Shanghai, and send me a few dollars every month.……"

Because I had something to do and had to come back, I couldn't listen anymore. On the way back, I thought: "I'm afraid that in a year, these examination candidates will come back wearing Western suits, and even the old examination candidates won't be able to recognize them."

— (Zhen)

In the face of carnal desires, reason is only a spark in a pile of rotten grass, how can it withstand the moon-like bright carnal fragrance and wine color?

A woman's heart is as soft as cotton wool when it is soft, and harder than iron when it is hard and unbending.

Ming Dynasty Restaurant 222

— Yanqiao

The sea breeze has swept through Nanjing, but only the south of the city still has some ancient charm. I wanted to taste a bit of "Nanjing flavor," so someone mentioned the Ming Dynasty Restaurant.

The Ming Dynasty Restaurant is located on Yuhua Road outside Zhonghua Gate, named "Ma Xiangxing," and is a complete halal restaurant. Its appearance is similar to that of the "Desolate Restaurant" in Suzhou. Upon entering, there is a stove, inside which people are sitting around tables drinking tea or sorghum liquor. However, those who come for the name generally take eating snacks as the principle. Noodles, dumplings, and pot stickers all use beef as the main ingredient. Its beauty lies in the perfect skill of the fire. The soup is mixed with chicken broth, especially the beef tendon, which is cooked very tenderly. It melts in your mouth and does not require chewing. This is one of the reasons why it has been famous for a long time. According to old diners, there is also a dish called "Stewed Something" (I have forgotten this special term), which is a unique flavor made by cooking the lower part of the cow's jaw until it is crispy and tender. They said they didn't have it that day, so it was a pity I couldn't try it.

Because of the good business, two elegant seats were opened on the left. Sun Zhesheng, the president of the Legislative Yuan, often patronizes the place. This year, Chu Minyi advocated flying kites, and Yuhuatai suddenly became crowded with people. Many people came to taste the "Ming Dynasty flavor," and the Ming Dynasty Restaurant was so crowded that people even took matters into their own hands and rushed to the cutting board to grab five-spice beef to eat.

Another point "that can show that they can maintain the ancient Chinese style is that everything is priced using 'cash codes.'" When we go to Qifang Pavilion to eat a bowl of clear tea, giving a small tip of five or six copper coins will make the waiter dissatisfied. However, the waiters at Ma Xiangxing don't care about these things. If you give a little more tip, they will smile and bow like shrimps to thank us.

Some say that this store was not founded in the Ming Dynasty but was founded by the current owner's great-grandfather, about 100 years ago. However, the poet Chen Shiyi has already been fooled, thinking that it is a real Ming Dynasty restaurant, so why should we be too serious and waste our time on research!

Reasons for Not Growing 223

— Shiying

Imperial Fragrance Adrift: A Record 224

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Unexpectedly, although Qing Shan's suggestion was to let the Empress Dowager rest in Tianjin, she could not accept his kindness. On the way, she declared that she wanted to rest. At that time, Qing Shan naturally dared not offer any more loyal advice, and the train stopped immediately. Here, not only was it not the big city that Qing Shan had imagined, nor was it in a small village, it was simply in a vast, uninhabited wilderness. But the Empress Dowager had absolutely not noticed this and only urged the eunuchs and maids to quickly put her quilts and pillows in order, and then she quietly went to sleep.

Our train actually had electric lighting equipment. The Empress Dowager did not have much affection for other new ideas or new devices, but she especially liked electric lights. In the palace and in the Summer Palace, there was a generator installed in each; therefore, she had come to regard electric lighting equipment as a necessary condition in daily life.

The news that the Empress Dowager had rested immediately gave the troops in the train following behind a considerable shock due to the sudden stop of our train; therefore, their train also stopped, about twenty or thirty feet away, stopping without a sound. Hundreds of imperial guards, wearing helmets and armor, and fully armed, quietly climbed out of the train and began to take on their responsibility of guarding. The surroundings of this yellow train were instantly filled with black shadows coming and going, and the flashing of swords. Especially on the left and right sides of the car that Emperor Guangxu was riding in, the guards were particularly strict; it would be more accurate to say that this special preparation was for the purpose of defending him rather than protecting Guangxu. Guangxu's plight was truly worse than that of any commoner, which I cannot help but point out again and again. (117)

A Small Contribution to Indicating Gender 225

— (Meixue)

Since each form has a gender column, it is of course very clear who is male and who is female. However, in the recent list of new students announced by various universities, which mostly admit both male and female students, it is not immediately clear to the outside world how many of the admitted new students are male and how many are female. This is a shortcoming in indicating gender.

Some say: "The signatures of women always carry a bit of femininity, so it is not necessary to indicate gender on the list, and people will naturally know." This statement is not correct. Recently, the names of female students have gradually become more masculine. Just by paying attention to the name, it is impossible to tell whether it is male or female. I think that if women call themselves "Ms." under their names, it seems a bit boastful and cannot be written on the exam paper, but it is okay to add a "Shi" character below the surname. With this identification, it will be clear at a glance whether it is male or female. Those with "Shi" are female, and those without "Shi" are male. According to this list on various forms, it is not necessary to add a gender item. When universities release the list according to this list, it will be clear who is male and who is female. The matter is very simple, why not adopt some of my small contributions?

Furthermore, adding "Shi" after a woman's surname is neither contrary to ancient teachings nor has the boastful nature of calling oneself "Ms." "Neither arrogant nor humble," it is also worthy of adoption by the women's world.

Short Story

Hometown 226

— Seqiu

When the train arrived at S City, I transferred to a small gasoline boat. With the sound of the leaves flapping, I left the pier and headed towards the future of my hometown.

Between spring and summer, the river water was rising, so soft and green! The boats in the river shuttled back and forth like shuttles, and the green fields on both sides reached directly to the sky. In the distance, I could vaguely see a distant mountain stretching into the clouds. "Oh, what a beautiful nature!" I couldn't help but walk out of the cabin, stand at the bow of the boat, and take a deep breath of fresh air.

I had been in the hustle and bustle of the city all day, my head dizzy from the foul air, and I couldn't get a moment of peace. I hadn't seen this kind of scenery in three years, and I felt an unspeakable joy in my heart. The small gasoline boat was dragging a very large barge behind it, so the speed couldn't be fast. It sailed slowly all the way. Looking down, the water in the river was clear enough to see the bottom. From time to time, countless fish were swimming back and forth in the water, so carefree and content. It has no ambition to invade others, and others do not invade it. It just lives a happy life leisurely.

From the voices of people on both sides of the river, I knew that I was getting closer and closer to my hometown. My heart felt sweet, sour, and bitter, and I didn't even know what it tasted like. Before long, my hometown, which I had dreamed of for so long, appeared before my eyes. The person who came to pick me up was also greeting me on the shore. At this time, the sun was gradually setting, and I only saw a red glow in the distance flying up to the sky, shining on the fields like blood. The guests in the boat walked out of the cabin one by one to go ashore. I also picked up my things and walked ashore, and slowly walked with the person sent by my family to pick me up. After turning a few bends in the fields, I arrived at X Town.

This small town has streets so narrow that they are almost as wide as the narrow alleys in the Shanghai Concession. The road surface is half dirt and half pebbles, and uneven in height. If it rains, it will be so muddy that it is impossible to walk. One side of the street faces the water. Although the river is small, there are many willows planted on both banks, constantly scratching their heads and making gestures in the wind, welcoming and sending off the passing boats. On the other side are shops. There are dozens of shops in a row, displaying various goods and waiting to be sold, including grain stores, foreign goods stores, and miniature department stores... These many shops all face the small river. Except for the morning vegetable market being a little more crowded, the streets are quiet and pedestrians are rare all day long. The staff in the shops sit in the cabinets all day long. They have neither radio to listen to like the stores in Shanghai nor do they have modern ladies to visit. With nothing to do all day long, they can only stare blankly at the boats coming and going in the shade of the trees opposite, and listen to the gentle rowing sounds. In fact, this kind of realm is not easy to obtain, but they are already tired of it, dreaming of the prosperity of Shanghai all day long.

"This is the one who came back from Shanghai." In each of their eyes, they expressed the psychology of envying Shanghai people. Going through an alley, the back is our hometown. At this time, my mother and daughter, as well as other relatives, came out with smiles and asked me why I came so late. My mother said: "The tomb has been built. Thanks to us coming back ten days earlier, we have arranged everything very comfortably. The coffins of your grandparents, which had been placed in the funeral home for a long time, were transported to the tomb yesterday. The burial day is the afternoon of the day after tomorrow. Your wife's coffin has just been transported from Shanghai. Probably the barge was too slow and delayed for so many days. It is temporarily placed in the funeral home. Since you have come down, you have to go see her."

I felt a pang of sadness and couldn't speak. I vaguely followed the person who was guiding me, staggering in the fields where the setting sun was about to end. After a few hundred steps, I could see the funeral home in front of me. At this time, my heart was filled with sadness, and I just lowered my head and followed the person in front of me. Walking to the door of several bungalows, the person guarding the funeral home opened the door and pointed with a smile at the one in the middle... God! Isn't that the shell of my wife sleeping there? At this time, the phantoms of three years ago jumped before my eyes, my eyes dizzy, and my ears were ringing endlessly. Wife! I wonder if you know that I have recently suffered even more of the tastes of the world? I held my heart with both hands, and I couldn't hold back the tears any longer.

In my confusion, I heard people say, "It's getting darker, let's go back!"

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

The Regeneration Movement of National Goods Industry 227

— Yang'an

Speaking with Tears

The news published in the newspaper every day is always about foreign goods being dumped and imports increasing sharply. Recently, a large amount of silver has been exported, and the cash reserves are drying up. Everyone says that they have suffered the pain of foreign goods selling well. National goods factories have reached this point. If they are not numb or insane, there will never be a situation of self-slaughter and infighting. But the business is not like this. There are still many factories that have forgotten the situation where the great enemy is in front of them and are surrounded by enemies on all sides, and they are still fighting desperately, not destroying industry rules, cutting prices to compete for sales, or producing shoddy goods and arbitrarily lowering prices. Industry associations have no legal means to sanction them; good-intentioned advice is also ignored. Like mad dogs, like insanity, the extreme is nothing more than harming others and not benefiting oneself, being jealous of others, and the result is perishing together, creating opportunities for foreign merchants. The ancients said that doing things should not cause pain to relatives but should bring joy to enemies. If there is such a situation among colleagues, whether it is for colleagues or compatriots, hearing this news is really very painful. However, the enemies of the neighbors celebrate every day and clap their hands from time to time, fearing that we are not like this. If there is some blood, some conscience, and some vision in any industry, they will never go straight to the end. There are not only the culprits, the scum, and the troublemakers of the industry. Judging from their intentions, they will not stop until the national goods disappear. They are true traitors, true social pests, and treacherous merchants who destroy the country and exterminate the race. Those who do not suffer human disaster will be punished by heaven. However, there is always justice in society, and there is right and wrong in the business world. For the current plan;

(1) Industry associations should be organized and powerful. Any industry that has such a situation should be severely sanctioned. Colleagues should not interact with each other, financial circles should cut off relations, and they should be expelled from the industry and not be in the same country as China.

(2) Industry associations should set prices and product grades. If a situation of price cuts or shoddy goods is discovered, it should be exposed and announced to the whole country immediately.

(3) Industry associations should invite technical experts to guide and organize each factory at any time, so that the products become more refined day by day to suit the tastes of users, and the cost is reduced to resist the invasion of foreign goods.

Recently, Shanghai National Goods organizations have seen this dangerous situation and proposed the establishment of a unified industry control committee to prevent price cuts and maintain the market. This view is very helpful for saving the country with national goods. I think there are many people in all industries who are deeply aware of justice. At this point, the rise and fall depend on one move. Only industry unity and cooperation can be possible, and it must not be taken lightly.

National Goods Proposals

Beggars Should Not Walk Side by Side 228

— Jingcun

"Beggars should not walk side by side" is a very common saying, and I would like to offer this sentence to those who are determined to start national goods factories.

Today, if we want to start a national goods factory, we must not forget a powerful enemy at the moment, which is the dumping of foreign goods. When resisting foreign aggression, we must pay attention to not creating internal conflicts again. If foreign aggression has not gone away and internal conflicts arise again, then the annihilation of the entire army is an expected thing. This very simple truth is known to everyone, but often many people forget this point due to being blinded by profit and suffer a miserable defeat.

Some say that our people are rich in imitation but lack creativity. This sentence seems to be somewhat true. Seeing that others have started a seasoning factory and made a profit, I also started a seasoning factory, you also started a seasoning factory, and he also started a seasoning factory. Seasonings filled the market, and the result was price competition, and in the future, they would all perish together. The rubber industry, enamel industry, thermos industry, and the emerging Bakelite industry all have this trend. If this dispersed power is concentrated, any strong enemy can be defeated. However, everyone does not think this way, and they act independently, and even compete with each other to reduce external strength. Isn't this digging one's own grave? Some say that there can be progress only if national goods production has more competition. I do not deny this sentence, but the object of competition is best to use foreign goods, and comparing competition with domestic products is not a hero, just like warlords who are brave in internal warfare and afraid of foreign wars, which is equally disgusting.

If I want to start a national goods factory, I must choose a business that the people of the country have not paid attention to. Perhaps my experience, knowledge, capital, and talent are suitable for running a certain national goods factory, and this factory is already being run by someone, I will completely contribute my experience, knowledge, capital, and talent to him, participate in the work, in order to increase his production capacity and strengthen his external strength, remembering "Beggars should not walk side by side," and also be sure to recognize the enemy, and not kill each other.

National Goods Talk

A Good Sign in the National Products Movement 229

— Ba Ling

Everyone knows that our Republic of China has truly reached a critical period of national crisis! While there are many reasons for this crisis, a major one is that most citizens are unwilling to use domestic products and instead act as promoters of foreign goods, causing domestic wealth to flow out, enriching foreigners while impoverishing our own people. Therefore, to resolve the national crisis and enable China to exist independently and freely in the world, we must make efforts in all aspects. However, promoting national products is undoubtedly one solution to this crisis, and this I can assert.

However, our Chinese national products movement has been promoted for quite a few years now. In theory, it should have achieved considerable success. Alas! The reality is that while proponents shout themselves hoarse, those who actually practice it are as rare as morning stars. From the perspective of those in the national products sector, this situation is deeply disheartening.

Why hasn't the promotion of national products yielded good results or significant achievements? While there are many reasons, I believe that the lack of governmental power to aid in its implementation is also a factor in the movement's failure to achieve results.

Now, things are looking up. On the 23rd of this month, I read in the newspaper that the Social, Education, and Public Safety Bureaus jointly discussed banning outlandish clothing. The regulations included not only strict orders to subordinates to ban outlandish clothing for both men and women but also strict orders that all men and women should, as much as possible, use domestic products when purchasing new clothing. The bureaus have drafted measures for the police to rigorously enforce. Upon reading this news, I couldn't help but applaud, recognizing it as a good sign for the future of our Chinese national products movement, worthy of endless praise.

This news makes me think that our Chinese authorities are now also vigorously promoting and enthusiastically supporting the national products movement. As the saying goes, "When those above cherish something, those below will cherish it even more." It is expected that with the government's vigorous promotion, the national products movement will undoubtedly achieve good results and significant accomplishments.

Finally, I especially hope that those compatriots who enjoy promoting foreign goods will quickly wake up! You must know that promoting national products is becoming a unanimous trend throughout the country. To violate this trend is to become a public enemy of the nation. "Public enemies" need to be compelled to use domestic products with political power. By that time, it will be too late for regrets.

National Product Introduction

Sichuan Crepe 230

— Wang Lun

Sichuan crepe, also known as Sichuan silk in Beiping, is one of the most famous silk fabrics in Chengdu. It is light, soft, dense, and very breathable when worn, and comes in a variety of vibrant colors. While its surface may not be as smooth and delicate as Hangzhou silk or spun silk, its material is more durable and its colors more wash-resistant than Hangzhou silk or spun silk.

Sichuan crepe can not only be used to make general summer clothing for both men and women but can also be used for autumn jackets and winter padded coats, making you feel light and warm.

In recent years, female students in large and medium-sized schools in Sichuan have been using crepe to make their everyday skirts because it is both economical and beautiful. It doesn't easily fray or snag even when worn daily. And when it gets dirty, you can take it off, wash it with boiling water, dry it in the sun, and iron it flat, making it look as good as new. As the autumn semester is about to begin, I would like to introduce Sichuan crepe to my fellow female students in secondary schools who are enthusiastically promoting national products.

Local Sichuan shops and the China National Products Company both sell Sichuan crepe.

Education News: Jiangsu Education Funds Borrowed 232

Half a Month Issued First, Half a Month Issued in Early September

Jiangsu education funds, after the end of the semester and at the beginning of the school year, when schools start, have mostly borrowed funds in previous years due to the transition period. Now, with the start of the school year and the urgent need for funds, the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office has followed the usual practice of borrowing from the Jiangsu, China, and Jiaotong banks, borrowing 80,000 yuan from Jiangsu, 70,000 yuan from China, and 50,000 yuan from Jiaotong, totaling 200,000 yuan (China has replied that they will borrow as planned; Jiangsu and Jiaotong have agreed that they can borrow as planned after reporting to their head offices). With the addition of funds in the treasury, issuing one month's funds to provincial education institutions and schools is no longer a problem. However, the borrowing is still being negotiated, and the funds have not been completely delivered to the treasury. It is calculated that the funds already delivered to the treasury are short by thirty to forty thousand yuan if half a month is issued first. Currently, the bank is requested to advance the full amount of the loan, which will be deducted from it in the near future. The Education Fund Management Office will issue payment notices to the schools on the 28th and 29th of this month (the rural teachers and primary schools will receive the first half of August's funds; social education, vocational schools, and normal schools will receive the second half of July's funds; and middle schools will receive the first half of July's funds), which will be sent to the schools and education institutions separately. The schools will receive the funds around the end of the month or the beginning of the next month. The payment notices for the second half of the month's funds (the second half of August's funds for rural teachers and primary schools, and so on) have already been stamped by the Jiangsu Education Fund Auditors Committee on the 25th of this month. The 26th and 27th are holidays. On the 28th, the Education Fund Office will send them to the Education Department for stamping. They will probably reach the schools in early September, and at that time, the bank loan can be completely delivered to the treasury. This second half of the month's funds can be paid around September 10th, it is said.

Jiangsu Education Fund: Tax on Livestock and Teeth Likely Not Mortgaged for Public Bonds 233

The Jiangsu Education Fund Office Requests the Provincial Government to Address Public Doubts

Jiangsu education funds use land tax and the tax on livestock and teeth as dedicated funds for education, and a special office is set up to manage them. The education funds are completely independent. Recently, the Education Fund Management Office sent an official letter to the Jiangsu Provincial Government regarding a report on August 21 stating that the Jiangsu Provincial Government planned to issue 30 million yuan in public bonds, with 14 million yuan earmarked for repaying old debts and 16 million yuan allocated to the Huai and Yun waterways projects and other uses. The guarantee fund would be the Jiangsu Province's stamp tax on brokerage and the salt surcharge, and the repayment period for the old debts would be extended by 19 years. However, these funds might not be sufficient, so in addition to the Huai and Yun waterways projects utilizing labor to save costs, the provincial government would allocate 300,000 yuan annually from the land tax to supplement them. The Executive Yuan had already submitted the case to the Ministry of Finance for review, and it was feared that these funds would not be sufficient to cover the costs. The letter explained that the tax on livestock and teeth had long been designated to be managed by the Management Office and earmarked for education, and could not be used as a guarantee fund for provincial public bonds. The office asked that the report, which it feared was a rumor, be verified and responded to, and that a correction be published in the newspaper to avoid confusing the public.

Record of the 11th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society (2) 234

Opening of the Annual Meeting: He Jian Speaks on the Economic Situation in Hunan Province

Shao Yuan Chong Speaks on Economic Control and Capacity Control

(Changsha Special Dispatch) The 11th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society was held at the Hunan University Library in Yuelu, Changsha, Hunan Province, on Sunday, the 26th of this month. The attendance of members at this year's annual meeting was very enthusiastic. The details of the opening ceremony are recorded below.

Members Present 235

The members who registered and participated in the opening ceremony of this year's annual meeting included Ma Yinchu, Shao Yuanchong, Gan Naiguang, Liang Hancao, Wang Yuxiang, Chen Changheng, Li Quanshi, Tang Qingzeng, Xu Zhaosun, Wang Keyou, Hu Songshan, Zhuang Zhihuan, Xu Jilian, Jin Guobao, Jiang Chanshan, Zeng Jixi, Liu Ziren, Xu Yao, Liu Junmu, Dong Qizheng, Pan Xulun, Xu Xinliu, Liu Tingzhuang, Dai Xiujun, Zhou Shizheng, Zhang Yuanjie, Wang Shude, Zhou Ren, Zhang Ningyi, Wu Juenong, Chen Guojun, Sheng Jun, and more than eighty others. The guests included He Yunqiao, Chairman of Hunan Province, Zhu Jingnong, Director of the Education Department, Zhang Kai𤧣, Director of the Finance Department, Hu Shuhua, President of Hunan University, and more than ten others.

Venue Arrangement 236

The opening ceremony of the 11th Annual Meeting of the Economic Society was held at the Hunan University Library at 3 p.m. on the 26th. Hunan University is located in the mountains of Yuelu, with beautiful scenery, especially the magnificent library building surrounded by greenery. The flags of the party and the nation were crossed at the entrance. There were registration desks for members and guests at the entrance. The portrait of the Prime Minister and the flag of the party and the nation were hung high in the center of the auditorium. The platform was decorated with potted flowers, and the front of the platform was the press seat, with the member seats in the front few rows and the guest seats in the back.

Chairman's Address 237

The opening ceremony of the annual meeting was chaired by Ma Yinchu, the president of the society. After the ceremony, the chairman stood up and reported the purpose of the meeting, saying that the Chinese Economic Society was initiated and organized in 1924 by Professor Taylor of Yenching University in Peking. At first, there were very few people, and it was just a discussion group. Later, it was expanded under the leadership of Mr. Liu Dajun, so Mr. Liu was the founder of the society. The society was first in the north and then moved to the south, and the number of members has increased with each year. In the past few years, annual meetings have been held in Shanghai, Wuxi, Hangzhou, Qingdao, and Nanjing. This year it is in Hunan, and next year it is scheduled to be in Sichuan. The reason why the annual meetings of the Economic Society must be held in various places is that the theory is connected with the facts. If the facts have no theory, it is easy to make mistakes, and if only theory is held and the facts are not considered, it is even easier to make mistakes. Therefore, the annual meetings of the society are held in various places to take this opportunity to visit and investigate the economic situation in various places and use it as a reference and goal for research. At present, one-third of the society's members are scholars, and two-thirds are from the banking industry. This trip is to admire the construction of Hunan and visit Hunan Province, which is to study China's economy today with Chinese economics. As for the society's funds, it currently has more than 100,000 yuan, most of which is helped by government banks and the industrial sector, so in the future, the society's members will serve the country and society with their collective strength. If the country is rich, our society will also prosper, and if the industries in various provinces develop, the society will inevitably develop along with it. Now Hunan has a large number of mineral deposits such as coal and antimony, which will become a rich province once developed. The society will do its best to help Hunan, and Hunan will benefit the society in the future. Finally, he said that Mr. Sun Zhesheng, who the society had invited, was in Honolulu to escape the summer heat and could not attend the meeting due to the long distance, and now he asked Chairman He for guidance.

He Jian's Speech 238

After the Chairman's report, He Jian stood up and gave a speech, saying that the 11th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society was held in Hunan this year, and Hunan would be able to gain many practical benefits after the meeting. Moreover, all the attendees are famous figures in China's academic circles and economic experts. The provincial government and the general headquarters welcome you all. Please take advantage of the opening day of your conference today to present the general economic situation of Hunan and the plans for future economic development to you all. Hunan Province has a land area of 692,000 square miles, and the climate is mild and pleasant, with no extreme heat in summer and no severe cold in winter. Dongting Lake is located in the northern part of the province, and tributaries are distributed throughout the province. The minerals produced include antimony, with a production of approximately 12,935 tons, accounting for the first place in the country, and zinc, which can reach 15,000 tons. In addition, coal, calcium, silver, and other minerals are also produced in large quantities in Hunan. Agricultural crops include rice, with a production of 107 million dan, cotton, with a production of 168,000 dan, tung oil, with a production of 398,000 dan, and black tea, with a production of more than 200,000 dan. The population is 302 million, and the people are mostly simple, sturdy and hardworking. From this point of view, it is not impossible to develop the rich resources of Hunan with the hardworking people of Hunan. In reality, Hunan, like China as a whole, has various difficulties that limit its development. From the 22nd year of Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty to the end of Xuantong, Chen Baozhen and Yu Lianxiang successively governed Hunan and tried to discuss ways to increase revenue and lay the initial economic foundation of Hunan. However, due to water and drought disasters, from the years of the Republic of China to the 23rd year, Hunan suffered seven floods and three droughts, averaging one disaster every two years. Then, it suffered military disasters. Since the beginning of the Republic of China, every time a war broke out, Hunan was involved in the vortex and sacrificed. Therefore, from the beginning of the Republic of China to the 19th year, there were almost continuous wars. Therefore, since the Republic of China, Hunan's finances have been short by a huge sum of 38,329,000 yuan. Therefore, from the beginning of the Republic of China to the 7th year, the price of banknotes fell strangely, and the financial system was in chaos. The inventory of money was more than 50,000 strings. Originally, one string was worth 7 jiao and 3 fen and 2 li of silver, but it fell to 1 jiao per string. Such a change is alarming. There is also the impact of the external economy on the economy of Hunan. According to recent statistics, imports of foreign goods accounted for 55%, with an average of 8.3 million taels of customs duties, and native goods accounted for 59%, with an average of 4.75 million taels of customs duties. Exports were only 7.56 million taels. This is also one of the obstacles to the economic development of Hunan. The financial impact and the economic panic in China also affected Hunan. The world economic panic after the 19th year also affected the whole of China and Hunan. Therefore, Hunan's economy is facing many difficulties, and the government is unable to do anything about it. From the perspective of history, the above-mentioned diseases have not been stable since the beginning of the Republic of China to the 20th year, and a large amount of cash has flowed out, as much as 28,213,600 taels. Therefore, Hunan can hardly see cash. The export goods of the industry, the Changsha Yuezhou Customs in the 21st year of the Republic of China had only 4,384,672 taels, which is a decrease of 50% compared with the 17th year of the Republic of China. The reason is political instability, and the economy has also suffered a lot of blows in these years. After the 19th year of the Republic of China, the transportation industry, which was working hard to develop the economy, has completed 1,200 miles of highways, and 1,187 miles of branch lines have been developed in five years. 920 miles of earth roads have been completed, for a total of 3,287 kilometers of highways. There are now 200 long-distance buses running, and a 1,000-watt radio station has been built, and there are already several places with radio receivers installed. In terms of industrial construction, there is the Hunan First Textile Factory, with 50,000 spindles, and the Hunan Machinery Factory, alcohol coal vehicles and porcelain improvement. In terms of agriculture, an agricultural experiment field has been established, with more than 400 mu of fields and more than 400 mu of tea land. The cotton experiment field has 100,000 mu of cotton planting land. There are also tea experiment fields, a forestry bureau, and a national products display hall has been established for commerce. Relief and water conservancy have been done to some extent in practice. Such small undertakings cannot be said to be construction, but in Hunan today, where financial resources are scarce, it is felt that the achievements have been made to the best of their ability. The way to develop in the future is to stabilize the people's hearts and work hard to eliminate the Communist bandits. The territory of Hunan Province is stable, and recently there have been bandits who have fled into the province. They have now been surrounded and will soon be eliminated. To develop the rich resources of Hunan, we can only develop the countryside, because developing the countryside is the only way out today. This is not only the case for Hunan Province, but the entire China also needs this kind of work. However, developing the countryside must rely on capital, so He Jian is very hopeful that the Shanghai banking industry will invest in Hunan with its concentrated savings in Shanghai.

Director Pan Presides, Mayor Wu's Representative Delivers a Training Speech

Enthusiastic Visitors Reached More Than 10,000 People Throughout the Day

Rich Exhibits, Especially the Most From Xinlu and Other Schools

Director Pan presided over the event, and Mayor Wu's representative delivered a training speech. The details are recorded below.

A Glimpse of the Venue 242

The venue is divided into two locations, Shangwen and Xicheng. There are more than 7,000 exhibits from all primary and secondary schools, divided into 18 categories: paper crafts, wax crafts, bamboo crafts, woodworking, metalworking, rattan crafts, embroidery, weaving, sewing, carving, stone carving, sculpture, clay crafts, plaster crafts, agricultural works, household goods, chemical crafts, and applied crafts. Exhibits from various schools are displayed in more than 20 rooms, filled with a wide variety of beautiful things. In the secondary school section, the machines of the China Vocational School are displayed in two rooms, making a great spectacle. The various specimens of Xinlu Normal School collected more than 400 pieces, which is very rich. The embroidery of female schools such as Wuben, Aiguo, Chengdong, and Shanghai Women's Middle School, the antique bronzes of Jingye, the stone carvings of Yangjing, and the educational supplies of Shanghai Middle School all have their own special achievements. In the primary school section, Shangwen has the most exhibits, with exquisite models of various transportation and military equipment and animal shapes. The National Defense Museum of He'an, the instruments of Wanzhu, the inscriptions and brick carvings of the Times, the bamboo carvings of Takahashi, the weaving of Qingxi, and the rattan crafts of Yangcun are also full of meaning. From 9 a.m. to 5 p.m., more than 10,000 teachers and students from the city's normal schools and schools in the southern district of Shanghai went to visit both venues. The Shangwen Boy Scouts and the Public Security Bureau sent police to the venue to provide services, so the order was very good.

Opening Ceremony 243

The opening ceremony was held at 9 a.m. Among those in attendance were Mayor's representative Zhang Yuanruo, City Party Department representative Li Erbai, guest Jiang Jianyu, and representatives of teachers and students from various primary and secondary schools, totaling more than 500 people. Director Pan presided over the meeting, Yuan Zengyu was the master of ceremonies, and Chen Yu and Li Kun were the recorders. The ceremony was performed as usual. First, Director Pan reported on the purpose of the meeting, followed by speeches by Secretary Zhang, the representative of the City Party Department, Li Erbai, and guest Jiang Wenyu. Chen Bai, the director of the meeting affairs, reported. Then, photos were taken and the ceremony was completed.

Director's Report 244

Director Pan's report briefly stated that today the Education Bureau is holding a preparatory exhibition of labor science achievements in primary and secondary schools in the city. The Ministry of Education will hold a national labor exhibition of primary and secondary schools, so it ordered each province and city to hold a preparatory exhibition first, select works, and send them to Beijing for display. The national exhibition has now been postponed to November. The city will hold an exhibition for three days starting today, divided into two parts. The secondary school section is in Shangwen, and the primary school section is in Xicheng. Compared with the number of primary and secondary schools in the city, the number of participants is certainly far from enough, but it is not bad to have so many schools participating in the first event. Because the Ministry of Education informed the provinces and cities that the exhibits must be sent to Beijing before September, and the preparation period coincided with the schools' vacation, there were fewer participants. Now, let me talk to you about the significance of labor. At present, labor science is a major subject in primary schools, and middle schools also attach importance to this part of the work. In the past, schools often focused on knowledge of writing, only knowing how to read with their brains and neglecting to use their hands and work to make things. Therefore, the current education is to remedy this shortcoming, so it pays attention to the combination of hands and brains. This is a trend in the change of direction of education. Why should there be this kind of change? Because everyone feels that the students trained by the schools are often unwilling to endure hardship and are prone to unemployment, so vocational education and production education are promoted to make students able to work and not suffer from unemployment panic. In order to inspect the labor achievements of primary and secondary schools, the Ministry of Education is holding an exhibition for mutual reference and observation and to seek improvement. I hope that the principals and students of each school will pay attention. All those who are engaged in labor science must understand that labor science focuses on labor work, not on books, and it is necessary to train students to be not afraid of labor work and give students the opportunity to do labor work. At present, each school lacks materials and there is no real achievement, and students do not regard labor as an important subject. It is hoped that each school will improve this.

Mayor's Address 245

Following this, Mayor Wu, representing Secretary Zhang, delivered a speech, stating that the Labor Exhibition held significant meaning, representing a shift in China's educational policy, and explaining the forward progress of Chinese national culture. He stated that Chinese history could be divided into two stages: one in the Yellow River basin and another in the Yangtze River basin. The Yellow River basin represented labor, while the Yangtze River basin represented non-labor, which was the cause of the decline of the Chinese nation. During the Yellow River period, both the upper and lower classes valued labor. The emperor made boats, carts, and palaces, which earned him the people's faith. Chinese culture then occupied an important position in the world. However, when the country moved to the Yangtze River basin, due to the self-importance of scholars, the so-called "scholars do not carry baskets, and successful candidates do not walk," a trend of non-labor was created, causing Chinese history to change direction. Until the end of the Qing Dynasty, general officials and gentry abolished the imperial examination system and created new schools to seek reform, but the result was the opposite. They were seduced by Western material civilization, and people's lives became more extravagant. Therefore, Chinese history was affected vertically by the non-labor trend of the Yangtze River basin, and horizontally by the seduction of Western material civilization, which brought the nation to its current state. Therefore, we must now create culture and improve people's lives by promoting labor, and restore China's inherent creative and scientific spirit so that culture can progress. Next, Li Erbai, the representative of the city's Party headquarters, gave a speech, followed by a speech from visiting guest Jiang Wenyu, and a report from Chen Bai, the director of the conference affairs, which were omitted.

Scheduled Judging 246

The entries have been evaluated by thirteen judges hired by the Municipal Education Bureau. The judging will begin on the morning of September 1st to select excellent products for display in Beijing. All other school entries must be collected from the school between 1:00 PM on September 1st and 12:00 PM on September 2nd. The school will not be responsible for storage after the deadline.

Dansu Section of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Plans to Establish a Sports Association 255

Changzhou Station is to be the site of the association to build a court, etc.

Employees of various departments in the Dansu section of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, in view of the lack of proper recreational venues during leisure time, recently resolved at a joint meeting of the section affairs to follow the successful precedents of Shangbei, Shangnan, Hangzhou, and Zhabei to establish a Dansu section sports association at Changzhou Station. The association will submit a request to the railway bureau for approval through each department, and the bureau will provide an annual subsidy of 250 yuan. First, a tennis court, soccer field, and basketball court will be built on vacant land near Changzhou Station, and a reading room and bathroom will be built to provide employees with recreational activities. The annual expenses will be limited to the bureau's subsidy and members' annual membership fees. The railway bureau is making great efforts to promote employees' sports and entertainment, and immediately approved the preparations. As for the subsidy, the bureau has drafted a comprehensive plan for employees' sports and entertainment, which will be approved when the plan is implemented.

Wu Bangwei's New Book "Volleyball Refereeing Method" Published 256

The first specialized work created in our country

Volleyball is the most interesting and popular team game, and it has a glorious history in our country and is now the most developed. However, the established volleyball rules are relatively simple. Not only is it easy to have different interpretations, but there are often disputes in competitions. In view of this, Wu Bangwei has drawn on his years of experience as a volleyball referee and specially wrote the book "Volleyball Refereeing Method." The book is rich in content and detailed in guidance. A summary is as follows: The book provides detailed instructions on the referee's preparation before the game, appointment, inspection, consultation, key points during the game, the duties of inspectors, recorders, and linesmen, as well as the serving mistakes under fouls and judgments, causing the ball to go out of bounds or hit into the opponent's zone from under the net, receiving or holding the ball, consecutive hits, touching the ball with the body or clothing below the buttocks, using assistance to jump and hit the ball, restrictions on the number of hits, touching the net, contact with the ball in the opponent's zone, obstructing off-court guidance, leaving the field without permission, delaying substitution procedures, incorrect behavior, mutual fouls, and serving order errors. The book is a thick volume in 32-open format, priced at 55 cents, with a special price of 10% off. The postage for mail order is 11 cents. The general distributor is the Qin Fen Bookstore at 392 Laoshenfu Road, French Concession, Shanghai, and 277 Sima Road. The bookstore's store also sells the book at the same price.

Page 17

Free Talk

Where Are the Great Works? 259

— Hun Ren

Where have the great works gone? To this question, I can answer without hesitation: The great works are in the wastepaper basket!

Some people will surely find my answer strange, and they will question me like this: There are so many large and small publications in the country, they need many articles, needless to say, as long as the work is valuable, are you still afraid of not having the opportunity to publish it?

Yes, this is the ideal of most people, but ideals and reality are two different things. The reality tells us: The editors of various publications all embrace the "Monroe Doctrine." Their territory - the publication - is used to solve the eating problems of their related relatives and friends. They are worried about "too many monks and not enough porridge," where can they spare a grain for others? Therefore, when your manuscript is sent to them, and they find that the manuscript is signed with the name of someone unrelated to them, they don't even bother to take a look and stuff it into the wastepaper basket.

It is so difficult to submit a casual manuscript, let alone publish a single book or collection. The bookstore owners are all extremely snobbish. They accept manuscripts based on "name." There is no problem in selling the copyright or collecting royalties for the manuscripts of famous writers. Many of them have already been reserved after just deciding on a book title, without knowing what the content is. However, they treat unknown writers whose status is below average very differently. When the manuscript seller approaches their desk, they size you up with their eyes hidden behind their glasses, then look at your rectangular newspaper package, and before you can open your mouth, they complain about a series of hardships - the book industry is in a slump, the countryside is bankrupt, losing money... and from time to time they add a few ha ha, hahaha... of sinister laughter, even more cruelly frightening, simply leaving the person standing next to him no chance to open his mouth.

The editors and bookstore owners are certainly to blame for the creation of this abnormal phenomenon, but the main reason is not entirely with them, but with the general blind readers, because they are a group of pitiful insects without any preconceived notions, holding the principle of only reading the works of famous writers. When the literary giants say that humorous articles are good, they read humorous magazines and books; when they say that sketches are good, they then choose to read sketches. In short, they say that literary giants’ farts smell fragrant. As for the works of unknown writers, they simply don't bother to take a look, as if it would be harmful to them after reading them. Bookstore owners are profit-oriented, and editors want their jobs to be stable, so they have to cater to the tastes of readers, specializing in publishing books by famous writers or inviting a few famous writers to be special writers to try to save face. In this way, the works of unknown writers are undoubtedly buried and silenced.

Although, we cannot say that the works of famous writers are all worthless, and the works of unknown writers are all great. The fact that famous writers can stand on the literary scene naturally means they have their skills. In addition, because of their deep experience and extensive reading, the works they write are of course not bad. However, because they are famous, bookstore owners come to reserve books one after another, and editors urge them to submit manuscripts every issue, so they are burdened with literary debts, but they have to perfunctorily deal with all parties. In this way, there are naturally very few brilliant works. Moreover, any famous writer has a limited number of great works in his life, and most of the great works are early works, because they became famous by relying on their early great works, in other words, by relying on their unknown works. From this point of view, the works of unknown writers cannot be ignored.

But what is the current situation? The great literary giants can only create perfunctory works; the contributors to various publications - those related to the editors - are only counting words, calculating how much money they can exchange for? The works of unknown writers can only be stuffed into the wastepaper basket. In this way, how can great works appear?

Many unknown writers, because there is no way to advance, those with ambition are angrily "throwing their pens to become farmers" or "throwing their pens to become workers." Those with weak wills go to the doors of literary giants, hoping to get their support. However, most literary giants want both fame and fortune, so where do they care about the life and death of others? As a result, the entire literary scene is filled with "smog"!

So I say that the great works are in the wastepaper basket, I am afraid I am not exaggerating!

What Kind of National Products Year Will Next Year Be Called? 260

— Bai Ge

Last year was called National Products Year, and this year is called Women's National Products Year. What is the reason for this?

I heard that the reason is very big, and there are many reasons: First, National Products Year was too general. The reason why National Products Year did not achieve results last year was because no one was specifically responsible. Naturally, this year the women's circle must take on the specific responsibility and start over. Second, women are the masters of household consumption, and many high-priced goods are consumed on their bodies. It is very good as long as they like to consume national products. In short, the main idea is that Women's National Products Year is actually much more practical and effective than National Products Year. Therefore, after National Products Year, there is another Women's National Products Year.

Isn't it like there is a what's girl's middle school or university after a what's middle school or university?

No, no, definitely not! That is a manifestation of a little bit of not recognizing women's personality. Women are social people just like men. Why are all the nouns that are common to everyone monopolized by men? For example, the distinction between he and she is an example. This is completely drawing women outside the general population and not treating women as social people. As for Women's National Products Year, it is different. It can be said that the meaning is completely opposite: it not only calls women to the society to become a social person, but also calls women to represent the general population to take on a part of the special responsibility of saving the country. This is such a worthy of joy thing! Therefore, since the new year came, here is also shouting Women's National Products Year, there is also shouting Women's National Products Year, as if everywhere is booming.

However, recently it seems that I have not smelled the boom. The results are probably still very good.

Um. According to the statistics recently released by the International Trade Bureau, it is like this: First, within six months of this year, the imported cosmetics and appliances consumed by women in our country are worth about 970,000 yuan. Second, the imported lace used by women to embroider cheongsams is worth about 600,000 yuan. Third, the imported spearmint gum consumed by Shanghai women in six months is worth about 238,000 yuan. Various other things that have not yet been published are probably also very considerable. Moreover, it is said that these imported consumables are mostly consumed by the aristocratic families and general fashionable women in Shanghai. However, weren't these women the ones who shouted Women's National Products Year before? It can be seen that these women's Women's National Products Year still has no results to speak of.

Then, next year, try using the laboring women who can only eat and dress and do not consume these consumables at all as representatives, and call it Laboring Women's National Products Year?

This, naturally, still has no results to speak of. First of all, these women will not do it like this. Whether other women want them to represent them is a secondary issue. However, the main problem lies here: if foreign rice, wheat, and cotton cloth are still pouring in, then soon not a bit of national product will be found on and in these women's bodies and stomachs. The resulting results are probably still the same as those obtained by women who apply cosmetics, wear lace, and chew spearmint. In fact, even what the current laboring women eat and wear is not mostly rice, wheat, and cotton cloth from the Great Republic of China, which is based on agriculture. In this way, it seems that no suitable person can be found to take specific responsibility for next year's National Products Year at all.

I think there are many National Products movers who are now hesitating about a question: What kind of National Products Year should next year be called?

Water Carrier 261

— Xi Jin

The city river has long looked at the sky,

The whole city panics about the drinking water problem!

The water carrier laughs in his belly,

You guys are unlucky, I am lucky!

The smiling face hung up a few days ago,

Is now gone;

The water carrier still has a bitter face,

Famine refugees also come to grab business!

Treading on the cracked bricks in the bottom of the algae-filled river,

He shakily carries two buckets of muddy water again;

"Come, come, to my house!"

The water carrier nodded and followed.

Wiping the sweat on his forehead,

The sweat on his back trickles down like insects crawling;

The floating grass knots in the water bucket keep spinning,

Is it really going to fall down?

Poor people will never have good days!

The water carrier keeps complaining about his unreliable waist and legs;

Under the baking sun,

The water carrier also hopes for rain like everyone else.

"Eventually everyone will die of thirst."

The water carrier is worried about the outer river becoming shallower and shallower;

The wealthy families have almost all run away to other places,

Business will be even more deserted day by day.

Poverty and Sickness (Continued Conclusion) 262

— Wu Mao

He settled me on the bed, then scrutinized me heavily again, shook his head, and sighed.

"This is no joke. You must go to the hospital quickly, Li!"

I still didn't speak, and closed my eyes.

"Go to the Red Cross Hospital, it's cheaper." It was Da's words again.

So, I slowly opened my eyes, looked at him, and asked:

"Why haven't the manuscript fees from X Bookstore been sent yet?"

He was stunned for a moment, then stammered:

"Yes, I was going to tell you, I went to the bookstore the day before yesterday to ask on your behalf, and they said they wouldn't use your manuscript. They said they were very sorry."

"Won't use it?" I almost shouted, but I didn't have the strength, and just glanced at him.

"Never mind if they don't use it," my friend consoled, continuing, "Go to the hospital today, okay?"

I glanced at him weakly again, without making a sound.

My friend seemed to finally understand my heart at this moment. He hesitated for a while, then asked:

"How much money do you have left? I have three dollars here. If it's not enough, take some clothes,..." He looked at me with feeling.

Instead, I gave a cold laugh. I didn't understand what I should do. I loved my life, but my only hope was cut off. I could only use my life to collide, to collide anywhere. I said resolutely:

"I have nothing, only that suit, you can take it."

He looked at me hesitatingly for a while, and finally stood up, "I'll go pawn it, we'll talk about it later if it's not enough."

He took my only property from the wall.

By the time he returned, it was already afternoon. As soon as he stepped into the door, he smiled bitterly at me, "Damn it, it's really worthless, only pawned for two dollars." After a while, without waiting for me to speak, he continued as if to comfort me: "It's almost enough, let's go to JX Hospital, you only need to pay a little money there. Let's go, I've already called a rickshaw at the door."

I should be grateful for Da's kindness. I also smiled bitterly and got out of bed, although I felt that poor people entering hospitals wouldn't cure their illnesses, I couldn't help but take a chance.

I held onto Da, went downstairs, and helped Da into the rickshaw.

Along the way, there was wind, there was sun, I lay straight in the rickshaw, my whole body seemed to be falling apart. The sky was spinning, the earth was spinning, everything was spinning....

However, I endured it, because I was going to the hospital.

The hospital's hideous iron gate was half-closed, the entrance was full of red and green paper, perhaps this was another grace of God, this hospital belonged to God.

Da helped me through the side door to the registration room. Before we could speak, a young man sitting at the entrance of the registration room stopped us and asked, "What do you want?"

"Register, see a doctor," Da replied.

"Special registration is five dollars."

"We want to register for a regular appointment."

"No, today is X holiday."

I don't know when I was spinning again in the wind and sun, I don't know when I lay down again in that gloomy attic, drowsily closing my eyes, all hope was gone.

Younger Brother (4) 263

— Zhou Wen

However, my younger brother's brute strength is sometimes very useful. Once, not far from the entrance, when I was being bullied by a classmate, I blushed and raised my hand, but this classmate was not afraid, and still stood directly in front of me, making many of the people around me laugh. But my younger brother came up wielding a large weighing pole, shouting loudly, and from afar, I could hear the clanging sound of the iron weighing hook hitting the weighing pole. That classmate turned tail and ran, and my younger brother chased after him for more than ten steps. The people watching naturally laughed again, but the meaning of this laughter was different from before.

Sometimes, in helplessness, my mother would stop the needlework in her hands, open her eyes with a faraway look, and murmur to herself, comforting herself:

"The fortune teller said that I will have good luck in ten years, and you two brothers are one civil and one military, ten years..."

Although it was ten years, the fleeting smile on my mother's lips seemed to indicate that it was not too long. However, after this, she felt that she had to send my younger brother to school no matter what. She would even lock him in school, and sit and wait for these "ten years"! After all, because of money, my younger brother and I could only each go to a different school, he was classmates with those barefoot children. In less than a year, I saw him read five copies of the Three Character Classic until they were worn out. How the teacher in that school taught, and how the students read, only God knows. When I came home on summer vacation from another county, I heard my mother say that the teacher liked to smoke opium, and my younger brother was often dragged back from the small river dripping wet.

The difference between high and low prices was 6 to 10 yuan, which was quite alarming.
